291	# Map each time slot to an index so we can do distance comparisons easily
292	TIME_INDEX: dict[str, int] = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
293	
294	
295	def score_schedule(schedule: Schedule) -> float:
296	    # Scores a single schedule and stores the result in schedule.fitness
297	    # Returns the fitness value. Higher is better.
298	    total = 0.0
299	
300	    # Counts how many times each facilitator appears at each time slot, and how many total activities they're assigned across the schedule
301	    fac_at_time:  dict[str, dict[str, int]] = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(int))
302	    fac_total:    dict[str, int]            = defaultdict(int)
303	    room_at_time: dict[str, dict[str, int]] = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(int))
304	
305	    for a in schedule.assignments:
306	        fac_at_time[a.facilitator][a.time] += 1
307	        fac_total[a.facilitator]           += 1
308	        room_at_time[a.room][a.time]       += 1
309	
310	    for a in schedule.assignments:
311	        cap    = ROOMS[a.room]
312	        enroll = a.activity.enrollment
313	
314	        # Room size scoring
315	        if cap < enroll:
316	            total -= 0.5
317	        elif cap > 3 * enroll:
318	            total -= 0.4
319	        elif cap > 1.5 * enroll:
320	            total -= 0.2
321	        else:
322	            total += 0.3
323	
324	        # Two activities booked in the same room at the same time
325	        if room_at_time[a.room][a.time] > 1:
326	            total -= 0.5
327	
328	        # Facilitator preference
329	        if a.facilitator in a.activity.preferred:
330	            total += 0.5
331	        elif a.facilitator in a.activity.other:
332	            total += 0.2
333	        else:
334	            total -= 0.1
335	
336	        # Facilitator load in this time slot
337	        if fac_at_time[a.facilitator][a.time] == 1:
338	            total += 0.2
339	        elif fac_at_time[a.facilitator][a.time] > 1:
340	            total -= 0.2
341	
342	    # Penalize or reward based on how many total activities a facilitator teaches
343	    for fac, count in fac_total.items():
344	        if count > 4:
345	            total -= 0.5
346	        elif count < 3:
347	            # Tyler is committee chair: no penalty if he has fewer than 2 activities
348	            if not (fac == "Tyler" and count < 2):
349	                total -= 0.4
350	
351	    # Activity-specific rules for the 101 and 191 sections
352	    by_name: dict[str, Assignment] = {a.activity.name: a for a in schedule.assignments}
353	
354	    sla101a = by_name.get("SLA101A")
355	    sla101b = by_name.get("SLA101B")
356	    sla191a = by_name.get("SLA191A")
357	    sla191b = by_name.get("SLA191B")
358	
359	    # The two SLA101 sections should be spread out
360	    if sla101a and sla101b:
361	        diff = abs(TIME_INDEX[sla101a.time] - TIME_INDEX[sla101b.time])
362	        if diff == 0:
363	            total -= 0.5
364	        elif diff >= 4:
365	            total += 0.5
366	
367	    # Same idea for the two SLA191 sections
368	    if sla191a and sla191b:
369	        diff = abs(TIME_INDEX[sla191a.time] - TIME_INDEX[sla191b.time])
370	        if diff == 0:
371	            total -= 0.5
372	        elif diff >= 4:
373	            total += 0.5
374	
375	    ROMAN_BEACH = {"Roman 201", "Roman 216", "Beach 201", "Beach 301"}
376	
377	    # Reward 101/191 pairs that run back-to-back, penalize if they overlap
378	    for s101 in filter(None, [sla101a, sla101b]):
379	        for s191 in filter(None, [sla191a, sla191b]):
380	            diff = abs(TIME_INDEX[s101.time] - TIME_INDEX[s191.time])
381	            if diff == 0:
382	                total -= 0.25
383	            elif diff == 1:
384	                total += 0.5
385	                # Penalize if one is in Roman/Beach and the other is not (widely separated buildings)
386	                if (s101.room in ROMAN_BEACH) != (s191.room in ROMAN_BEACH):
387	                    total -= 0.4
388	            elif diff == 2:
389	                total += 0.25
390	
391	    # Penalize facilitators with consecutive time slots if their rooms are in different buildings
392	    # (Roman/Beach vs everything else) — same rule as 101/191 consecutive building mismatch
393	    fac_rooms: dict[str, dict[str, str]] = defaultdict(dict)
394	    for a in schedule.assignments:
395	        fac_rooms[a.facilitator][a.time] = a.room
396	
397	    for fac in fac_rooms:
398	        slots = sorted(fac_rooms[fac].keys(), key=lambda t: TIME_INDEX[t])
399	        for i in range(len(slots) - 1):
400	            if TIME_INDEX[slots[i + 1]] - TIME_INDEX[slots[i]] == 1:
401	                room_a = fac_rooms[fac][slots[i]]
402	                room_b = fac_rooms[fac][slots[i + 1]]
403	                if (room_a in ROMAN_BEACH) != (room_b in ROMAN_BEACH):
404	                    total -= 0.4
405	
406	    schedule.fitness = total
407	    return total
408	
409	
410	def score_population(population: list[Schedule]) -> None:
411	    # Scores every schedule in the population (mutates in place)
412	    for s in population:
413	        score_schedule(s)
414	
415	
416	def population_stats(population: list[Schedule]) -> dict:
417	    # Returns best, worst, average fitness and references to the best/worst schedules
418	    scored = [s for s in population if s.fitness is not None]
419	    if not scored:
420	        return {}
421	    fitnesses   = [s.fitness for s in scored]
422	    best_sched  = max(scored, key=lambda s: s.fitness)
423	    worst_sched = min(scored, key=lambda s: s.fitness)
424	    return {
425	        "best":        best_sched.fitness,
426	        "worst":       worst_sched.fitness,
427	        "average":     sum(fitnesses) / len(fitnesses),
428	        "best_sched":  best_sched,
429	        "worst_sched": worst_sched,
430	        "count":       len(scored),
431	    }
432	
433	
434	def print_stats(stats: dict, generation: int = 0, prev_best: float = None) -> None:
435	    # Prints a one-line summary for a generation; shows % improvement if prev_best is given
436	
437	    # NOTE: % improvement will be blank at generation 0 b/c there is nothing to compare to yet. It will start showing once Part 3's evolution loop runs and passes the previous generation's best fitness into prev_best each iteration
438	
439	    pct_str = ""
440	    if prev_best is not None and prev_best != 0:
441	        improvement = (stats["best"] - prev_best) / abs(prev_best) * 100
442	        pct_str = f"  |  Improvement: {improvement:+.2f}%"
443	
444	    print(
445	        f"  Gen {generation:>4}  |  "
446	        f"Best: {stats['best']:>8.4f}  |  "
447	        f"Worst: {stats['worst']:>8.4f}  |  "
448	        f"Avg: {stats['average']:>8.4f}"
449	        + pct_str
450	    )
451	
452	# End of Part 2
453	
454	
455	# Start of Part 3: Genetic Algorithm (NumPy-vectorized)
456	
457	
458	# Index maps and lookup tables (built once at startup)
459	TIME_TO_IDX: dict[str, int] = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
460	ROOM_TO_IDX: dict[str, int] = {r: i for i, r in enumerate(ROOMS)}
461	FAC_TO_IDX:  dict[str, int] = {f: i for i, f in enumerate(FACILITATORS)}
462	ACT_NAMES:   list[str]      = [a["name"] for a in ACTIVITIES_DEF]
463	
464	N_TIMES = len(TIMES)
465	N_ROOMS = len(ROOMS)
466	N_FACS  = len(FACILITATORS)
467	N_ACTS  = len(ACTIVITIES_DEF)
468	
469	ROOM_CAPACITY       = np.array(list(ROOMS.values()), dtype=np.int64)
470	ACTIVITY_ENROLLMENT = np.array([a["enrollment"] for a in ACTIVITIES_DEF], dtype=np.int64)
471	
472	# (11, 10) facilitator score: +0.5 preferred, +0.2 other, -0.1 neither.
473	# `other` is written first so `preferred` overwrites duplicates (e.g. SLA449 lists
474	# Zeldin in both) — matches score_schedule's if/elif order.
475	FAC_SCORE = np.full((N_ACTS, N_FACS), -0.1, dtype=np.float64)
476	for _a_idx, _act in enumerate(ACTIVITIES_DEF):
477	    for _f in _act["other"]:
478	        FAC_SCORE[_a_idx, FAC_TO_IDX[_f]] = 0.2
479	    for _f in _act["preferred"]:
480	        FAC_SCORE[_a_idx, FAC_TO_IDX[_f]] = 0.5
481	
482	ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS = np.array(
483	    [name.startswith(("Roman", "Beach")) for name in ROOMS],
484	    dtype=bool,
485	)
486	
487	IDX_101A = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA101A")
488	IDX_101B = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA101B")
489	IDX_191A = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA191A")
490	IDX_191B = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA191B")
491	TYLER_IDX = FAC_TO_IDX["Tyler"]
492	
493	PAIR_I, PAIR_J = np.triu_indices(N_ACTS, k=1)   # 55 pairs
494	
495	_GA_RNG: Generator = Generator(PCG64DXSM())
496	
497	
498	def random_population_array(n: int, rng: Optional[Generator] = None) -> np.ndarray:
499	    # Generate n random schedules as a single (n, 11, 3) int array.
500	    if rng is None:
501	        rng = _GA_RNG
502	    pop = np.empty((n, N_ACTS, 3), dtype=np.int64)
503	    pop[:, :, 0] = rng.integers(0, N_TIMES, size=(n, N_ACTS))
504	    pop[:, :, 1] = rng.integers(0, N_ROOMS, size=(n, N_ACTS))
505	    pop[:, :, 2] = rng.integers(0, N_FACS,  size=(n, N_ACTS))
506	    return pop
507	
508	
509	def row_to_schedule(row: np.ndarray) -> Schedule:
510	    # Convert a (11, 3) genome row into a Schedule dataclass (for printing).
511	    assignments = []
512	    for a_idx in range(N_ACTS):
513	        t_idx = int(row[a_idx, 0])
514	        r_idx = int(row[a_idx, 1])
515	        f_idx = int(row[a_idx, 2])
516	        assignments.append(Assignment(
517	            activity=ACTIVITY_DEFS[a_idx],
518	            room=ROOM_NAMES[r_idx],
519	            time=TIMES[t_idx],
520	            facilitator=FACILITATORS[f_idx],
521	        ))
522	    return Schedule(assignments=assignments)
523	
524	
525	def score_batch(pop: np.ndarray, return_breakdown: bool = False):
526	    # Vectorized fitness for an (M, 11, 3) population.
527	    # Mirrors score_schedule exactly (verified by parity_test).
528	    # If return_breakdown=True, also returns a dict mapping component name to (M,) array.
529	    M = pop.shape[0]
530	    times = pop[:, :, 0]
531	    rooms = pop[:, :, 1]
532	    facs  = pop[:, :, 2]
533	
534	    # Room size rubric
535	    cap = ROOM_CAPACITY[rooms]
536	    enr = ACTIVITY_ENROLLMENT[None, :]
537	    room_score = np.where(
538	        cap < enr, -0.5,
539	        np.where(cap > 3 * enr, -0.4,
540	        np.where(cap > 1.5 * enr, -0.2, 0.3))
541	    )
542	    room_total = room_score.sum(axis=1)
543	
544	    # Same-time-same-room collisions (any colliding activity: -0.5)
545	    same_time = times[:, PAIR_I] == times[:, PAIR_J]
546	    same_room = rooms[:, PAIR_I] == rooms[:, PAIR_J]
547	    collides  = same_time & same_room
548	    counts = np.zeros((M, N_ACTS), dtype=np.int64)
549	    np.add.at(counts, (slice(None), PAIR_I), collides.astype(np.int64))
550	    np.add.at(counts, (slice(None), PAIR_J), collides.astype(np.int64))
551	    collision_total = (-0.5 * (counts > 0).astype(np.float64)).sum(axis=1)
552	
553	    # Facilitator preference (per-activity lookup)
554	    act_idx = np.arange(N_ACTS)[None, :]
555	    fac_pref_total = FAC_SCORE[act_idx, facs].sum(axis=1)
556	
557	    # Facilitator load per (time, fac)
558	    ft_counts = np.zeros((M, N_TIMES, N_FACS), dtype=np.int64)
559	    np.add.at(ft_counts, (np.arange(M)[:, None], times, facs), 1)
560	    shared = ft_counts[np.arange(M)[:, None], times, facs]
561	    fac_load_total = np.where(shared == 1, 0.2, -0.2).sum(axis=1)
562	
563	    # Global facilitator totals (-0.5 if >4; -0.4 if <3 with Tyler exemption for <2)
564	    f_totals = ft_counts.sum(axis=1)
565	    over_4 = f_totals > 4
566	    under_3 = (f_totals > 0) & (f_totals < 3)
567	    tyler_col = (f_totals[:, TYLER_IDX] >= 2) & (f_totals[:, TYLER_IDX] < 3)
568	    under_3[:, TYLER_IDX] = tyler_col
569	    fac_global_total = -0.5 * over_4.sum(axis=1) - 0.4 * under_3.sum(axis=1)
570	
571	    # SLA 101A vs 101B
572	    d = np.abs(times[:, IDX_101A] - times[:, IDX_101B])
573	    sla_101_total = np.where(d == 0, -0.5, 0.0) + np.where(d >= 4, 0.5, 0.0)
574	
575	    # SLA 191A vs 191B
576	    d = np.abs(times[:, IDX_191A] - times[:, IDX_191B])
577	    sla_191_total = np.where(d == 0, -0.5, 0.0) + np.where(d >= 4, 0.5, 0.0)
578	
579	    # Cross 101 x 191 pairs
580	    sla_cross_total = np.zeros(M, dtype=np.float64)
581	    pairs_101 = [IDX_101A, IDX_101A, IDX_101B, IDX_101B]
582	    pairs_191 = [IDX_191A, IDX_191B, IDX_191A, IDX_191B]
583	    for a_i, a_j in zip(pairs_101, pairs_191):
584	        t_a = times[:, a_i]; t_b = times[:, a_j]
585	        r_a = rooms[:, a_i]; r_b = rooms[:, a_j]
586	        d = np.abs(t_a - t_b)
587	        sla_cross_total += np.where(d == 0, -0.25, 0.0)
588	        sla_cross_total += np.where(d == 1,  0.5,  0.0)
589	        sla_cross_total += np.where(d == 2,  0.25, 0.0)
590	        consec = (d == 1)
591	        rb_a = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_a]
592	        rb_b = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_b]
593	        mismatch = consec & (rb_a != rb_b)
594	        sla_cross_total += np.where(mismatch, -0.4, 0.0)
595	
596	    # Facilitator consecutive slots with building mismatch (-0.4 per occurrence).
597	    # Mirrors score_schedule quirk: last activity in activity-order wins the (time, fac) slot.
598	    fac_room_at_time = np.full((M, N_TIMES, N_FACS), -1, dtype=np.int64)
599	    row_idx = np.arange(M)
600	    for act_i in range(N_ACTS):
601	        fac_room_at_time[row_idx, times[:, act_i], facs[:, act_i]] = rooms[:, act_i]
602	    occupied = fac_room_at_time >= 0
603	    fac_consec_total = np.zeros(M, dtype=np.float64)
604	    for t_slot in range(N_TIMES - 1):
605	        both = occupied[:, t_slot, :] & occupied[:, t_slot + 1, :]
606	        r_a = np.where(both, fac_room_at_time[:, t_slot,     :], 0)
607	        r_b = np.where(both, fac_room_at_time[:, t_slot + 1, :], 0)
608	        rb_a = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_a]
609	        rb_b = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_b]
610	        mismatch = both & (rb_a != rb_b)
611	        fac_consec_total += -0.4 * mismatch.sum(axis=1)
612	
613	    fitness = (
614	        room_total + collision_total + fac_pref_total + fac_load_total
615	        + fac_global_total + sla_101_total + sla_191_total
616	        + sla_cross_total + fac_consec_total
617	    )
618	
619	    if return_breakdown:
620	        breakdown = {
621	            "room size":       room_total,
622	            "collisions":      collision_total,
623	            "fac preference":  fac_pref_total,
624	            "fac load (slot)": fac_load_total,
625	            "fac totals":      fac_global_total,
626	            "SLA 101 split":   sla_101_total,
627	            "SLA 191 split":   sla_191_total,
628	            "SLA 101×191":     sla_cross_total,
629	            "fac consecutive": fac_consec_total,
630	        }
631	        return fitness, breakdown
632	    return fitness
633	
634	
635	def parity_test(n: int = 200, seed: int = 0) -> None:
636	    # Assert score_batch matches score_schedule on n random schedules.
637	    rng = Generator(PCG64DXSM(seed=seed))
638	    pop = random_population_array(n, rng=rng)
639	    vec_scores = score_batch(pop)
640	    for i in range(n):
641	        ref = score_schedule(row_to_schedule(pop[i]))
642	        if not np.isclose(vec_scores[i], ref, atol=1e-9):
643	            print(f"Parity mismatch at i={i}: vec={vec_scores[i]} ref={ref}")
644	            print(f"  genome: {pop[i].tolist()}")
645	            raise AssertionError("score_batch does not match score_schedule")
646	    print(f"Parity test passed ({n} schedules).")
647	
648	
649	def crossover_batch(parents_a: np.ndarray, parents_b: np.ndarray,
650	                    rng: Generator) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
651	    # Per-field coin-flip crossover. Returns two child arrays, each (P, 11, 3).
652	    mask = rng.random((parents_a.shape[0], N_ACTS, 3)) < 0.5
653	    child1 = np.where(mask, parents_a, parents_b).astype(np.int64, copy=False)
654	    child2 = np.where(mask, parents_b, parents_a).astype(np.int64, copy=False)
655	    return child1, child2
656	
657	
658	def mutate_batch(genomes: np.ndarray, rate: float, rng: Generator) -> None:
659	    # In-place per-gene mutation. Replaces fields with fresh domain draws.
660	    n = genomes.shape[0]
661	    mask = rng.random((n, N_ACTS, 3)) < rate
662	    if not mask.any():
663	        return
664	    replacements = np.empty_like(genomes)
665	    replacements[:, :, 0] = rng.integers(0, N_TIMES, size=(n, N_ACTS))
666	    replacements[:, :, 1] = rng.integers(0, N_ROOMS, size=(n, N_ACTS))
667	    replacements[:, :, 2] = rng.integers(0, N_FACS,  size=(n, N_ACTS))
668	    genomes[mask] = replacements[mask]
669	
670	
671	def choose_pair_indices(elite_fitness: np.ndarray, n_pairs: int,
672	                        rng: Generator) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
673	    # Softmax-weighted sampling within the elite block, with replacement across pairs.
674	    shifted = elite_fitness - elite_fitness.max()
675	    probs = np.exp(shifted)
676	    probs /= probs.sum()
677	    picks = rng.choice(len(elite_fitness), size=n_pairs * 2, replace=True, p=probs)
678	    a_idx = picks[0::2].copy()
679	    b_idx = picks[1::2].copy()
680	    dup = a_idx == b_idx
681	    while dup.any():
682	        b_idx[dup] = rng.choice(len(elite_fitness), size=int(dup.sum()), p=probs)
683	        dup = a_idx == b_idx
684	    return a_idx, b_idx
685	
686	
687	def _gen_line(gen: int, best: float, avg: float, worst: float,
688	              delta_pct: Optional[float], rate: float) -> str:
689	    d = f"{delta_pct:+7.2f}%" if delta_pct is not None else "   —   "
690	    return (f"G {gen:>4} | best={best:7.3f} | avg={avg:7.3f} | "
691	            f"worst={worst:7.3f} | Δavg={d} | λ={rate:.5f}")
692	
693	
694	def write_best_schedule(row: np.ndarray, fitness: float,
695	                        path: str = BEST_SCHEDULE_FILE) -> None:
696	    sched = row_to_schedule(row)
697	    sched.fitness = fitness
698	    time_order = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
699	    assignments = sorted(sched.assignments,
700	                         key=lambda a: (time_order[a.time], a.activity.name))
701	    lines = [
702	        f"Best schedule — fitness = {fitness:.4f}",
703	        "",
704	        f"{'Activity':<10}  {'Time':<6}  {'Room':<12}  {'Facilitator':<12}  {'Enroll':>6}  {'Cap':>4}",
705	        "-" * 60,
706	    ]
707	    prev_time: Optional[str] = None
708	    for a in assignments:
709	        if prev_time is not None and a.time != prev_time:
710	            lines.append("")
711	        prev_time = a.time
712	        lines.append(
713	            f"{a.activity.name:<10}  {a.time:<6}  {a.room:<12}  "
714	            f"{a.facilitator:<12}  {a.activity.enrollment:>6}  {ROOMS[a.room]:>4}"
715	        )
716	    Path(path).write_text("\n".join(lines) + "\n")
717	    print(f"Wrote best schedule → {path}")
718	
719	
720	def write_history_csv(history: list[dict], path: str = FITNESS_HISTORY_CSV) -> None:
721	    with open(path, "w", newline="") as f:
722	        w = csv.writer(f)
723	        w.writerow(["gen", "best", "avg", "worst", "delta_pct", "lambda"])
724	        for h in history:
725	            w.writerow([
726	                h["gen"], h["best"], h["avg"], h["worst"],
727	                "" if h["delta_pct"] is None else h["delta_pct"],
728	                h["rate"],
729	            ])
730	    print(f"Wrote fitness history → {path}")
731	
732	
733	class Visualizer:
734	    # Live 6-panel matplotlib view that refreshes each generation.
735	    # Lazily imports matplotlib so the module can run headless without it.
736	    def __init__(self) -> None:
737	        try:
738	            import matplotlib
739	            import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
740	        except ImportError as e:
741	            raise RuntimeError(
742	                "matplotlib is required for --viz. Install with: pip install matplotlib"
743	            ) from e
744	        self._plt = plt
745	        plt.ion()
746	        self.fig, self.axes = plt.subplots(2, 3, figsize=(16, 9))
747	        self.fig.suptitle("GA live visualization", fontsize=14)
748	        try:
749	            self.fig.canvas.manager.set_window_title("GA Live")
750	        except Exception:
751	            pass
752	        plt.show(block=False)
753	
754	    def on_gen(self, history: list[dict], pop: np.ndarray, fitness: np.ndarray,
755	               rate: float, halving_gens: list[int]) -> None:
756	        axes = self.axes
757	        best_i = int(np.argmax(fitness))
758	        best_row = pop[best_i]
759	        gens = [h["gen"] for h in history]
760	
761	        # (0,0) fitness over generations + halving markers
762	        ax = axes[0, 0]; ax.clear()
763	        ax.plot(gens, [h["best"]  for h in history], label="best",  color="#1f77b4")
764	        ax.plot(gens, [h["avg"]   for h in history], label="avg",   color="#2ca02c")
765	        ax.plot(gens, [h["worst"] for h in history], label="worst", color="#d62728")
766	        for g in halving_gens:
767	            ax.axvline(g, color="orange", linestyle="--", alpha=0.6, linewidth=1)
768	        ax.set_title("Fitness over generations")
769	        ax.set_xlabel("generation"); ax.set_ylabel("fitness")
770	        ax.legend(loc="lower right"); ax.grid(alpha=0.3)
771	
772	        # (0,1) lambda schedule
773	        ax = axes[0, 1]; ax.clear()
774	        rates = [h["rate"] for h in history]
775	        ax.step(gens, rates, where="post", color="orange")
776	        ax.set_yscale("log")
777	        ax.set_title("Mutation rate λ"); ax.set_xlabel("generation")
778	        ax.set_ylabel("λ (log)"); ax.grid(alpha=0.3)
779	
780	        # (0,2) constraint breakdown of current best
781	        ax = axes[0, 2]; ax.clear()
782	        _, breakdown = score_batch(best_row[None, :, :], return_breakdown=True)
783	        labels = list(breakdown.keys())
784	        values = [float(breakdown[k][0]) for k in labels]
785	        colors = ["#2ca02c" if v >= 0 else "#d62728" for v in values]
786	        ax.barh(labels, values, color=colors)
787	        ax.axvline(0, color="black", linewidth=0.5)
788	        ax.set_title(f"Best breakdown (total = {float(fitness[best_i]):.2f})")
789	        ax.set_xlabel("points"); ax.invert_yaxis()
790	
791	        # (1,0) facilitator load of current best
792	        ax = axes[1, 0]; ax.clear()
793	        counts = np.bincount(best_row[:, 2], minlength=N_FACS)
794	        bar_colors = []
795	        for f_i, c in enumerate(counts):
796	            if c > 4:
797	                bar_colors.append("#d62728")
798	            elif c < 3 and not (f_i == TYLER_IDX and c < 2):
799	                bar_colors.append("#ff7f0e")
800	            else:
801	                bar_colors.append("#2ca02c")
802	        ax.bar(FACILITATORS, counts, color=bar_colors)
803	        ax.axhline(3, color="gray", linestyle=":", alpha=0.6)
804	        ax.axhline(4, color="gray", linestyle=":", alpha=0.6)
805	        ax.set_title("Facilitator load (best)"); ax.set_ylabel("# activities")
806	        ax.tick_params(axis="x", rotation=30)
807	
808	        # (1,1) room utilization of current best
809	        ax = axes[1, 1]; ax.clear()
810	        slot_counts = np.bincount(best_row[:, 1], minlength=N_ROOMS)
811	        ax.bar(ROOM_NAMES, slot_counts, color="#1f77b4")
812	        ax.set_title("Room utilization (best)"); ax.set_ylabel("activities scheduled")
813	        ax.tick_params(axis="x", rotation=30)
814	
815	        # (1,2) time x room heatmap — visualizes same-time-same-room collisions
816	        ax = axes[1, 2]; ax.clear()
817	        heat = np.zeros((N_TIMES, N_ROOMS), dtype=int)
818	        for t, r in zip(best_row[:, 0], best_row[:, 1]):
819	            heat[t, r] += 1
820	        ax.imshow(heat, aspect="auto", cmap="YlOrRd", vmin=0, vmax=max(2, heat.max()))
821	        ax.set_xticks(range(N_ROOMS)); ax.set_xticklabels(ROOM_NAMES, rotation=30, ha="right")
822	        ax.set_yticks(range(N_TIMES)); ax.set_yticklabels(TIMES)
823	        ax.set_title("Time × room (best)")
824	        for (y, x), v in np.ndenumerate(heat):
825	            if v > 0:
826	                ax.text(x, y, str(v), ha="center", va="center",
827	                        color="black" if v < 2 else "white", fontsize=8)
828	
829	        self.fig.tight_layout(rect=[0, 0, 1, 0.96])
830	        self._plt.pause(0.001)
831	
832	    def close(self, block: bool = True) -> None:
833	        self._plt.ioff()
834	        if block:
835	            self._plt.show()
836	
837	
838	def run_ga(pop_size: int = POPULATION_SIZE,
839	           elite_count: int = ELITE_COUNT,
840	           pair_count: int  = PAIR_COUNT,
841	           initial_rate: float = MUTATION_RATE,
842	           min_generations: int = MIN_GENERATIONS,
843	           max_generations: Optional[int] = None,
844	           seed: Optional[int] = None,
845	           verbose: bool = True,
846	           visualizer: Optional[Visualizer] = None,
847	           write_outputs: bool = True) -> dict:
848	    # Main GA loop. Returns the final history snapshot (best-so-far at termination).
849	    rng = Generator(PCG64DXSM(seed=seed)) if seed is not None else _GA_RNG
850	
851	    def say(msg: str) -> None:
852	        if verbose:
853	            print(msg)
854	
855	    if verbose:
856	        say("Parity test: score_batch vs score_schedule …")
857	        parity_test(200)
858	
859	    say(f"Generating initial population of {pop_size} …")
860	    pop = random_population_array(pop_size, rng)
861	    fitness = score_batch(pop)
862	
863	    rate = initial_rate
864	    history: list[dict] = []
865	    halving_gens: list[int] = []
866	    halvings = 0
867	    last_halve_gen = 0
868	    streak = 0
869	
870	    def snapshot(gen: int, delta_pct: Optional[float]) -> None:
871	        best_i = int(np.argmax(fitness))
872	        stats = {
873	            "gen": gen,
874	            "best":  float(fitness.max()),
875	            "avg":   float(fitness.mean()),
876	            "worst": float(fitness.min()),
877	            "delta_pct": delta_pct,
878	            "rate": rate,
879	            "best_row": pop[best_i].copy(),
880	        }
881	        history.append(stats)
882	        if verbose:
883	            print(_gen_line(gen, stats["best"], stats["avg"], stats["worst"], delta_pct, rate))
884	
885	    snapshot(0, None)
886	    if visualizer is not None:
887	        visualizer.on_gen(history, pop, fitness, rate, halving_gens)
888	
889	    for gen in itertools.count(1):
890	        elite_idx = np.argpartition(fitness, -elite_count)[-elite_count:]
891	        elite_pop = pop[elite_idx]
892	        elite_fit = fitness[elite_idx]
893	
894	        a_idx, b_idx = choose_pair_indices(elite_fit, pair_count, rng)
895	        c1, c2 = crossover_batch(elite_pop[a_idx], elite_pop[b_idx], rng)
896	        offspring = np.concatenate([c1, c2], axis=0)
897	        mutate_batch(offspring, rate, rng)
898	        off_fit = score_batch(offspring)
899	
900	        pop     = np.concatenate([elite_pop, offspring], axis=0)
901	        fitness = np.concatenate([elite_fit,  off_fit],  axis=0)
902	
903	        prev_avg = history[-1]["avg"]
904	        denom = abs(prev_avg) if prev_avg != 0 else 1.0
905	        delta_pct = 100.0 * (fitness.mean() - prev_avg) / denom
906	        snapshot(gen, delta_pct)
907	
908	        assert pop.shape == (pop_size, N_ACTS, 3), f"bad pop shape {pop.shape}"
909	        assert fitness.shape == (pop_size,), f"bad fitness shape {fitness.shape}"
910	        assert not np.isnan(fitness).any(), "fitness contains NaN"
911	
912	        if visualizer is not None:
913	            visualizer.on_gen(history, pop, fitness, rate, halving_gens)
914	
915	        if max_generations is not None and gen >= max_generations:
916	            say(f"--- hit max_generations={max_generations}, stopping ---")
917	            break
918	
919	        if gen < min_generations:
920	            continue
921	
922	        if delta_pct < IMPROVEMENT_THRESHOLD * 100:
923	            streak += 1
924	        else:
925	            streak = 0
926	
927	        if streak >= PLATEAU_DEBOUNCE and (gen - last_halve_gen) >= HALVING_COOLDOWN:
928	            if halvings < MAX_HALVINGS:
929	                rate /= 2.0
930	                halvings += 1
931	                last_halve_gen = gen
932	                halving_gens.append(gen)
933	                streak = 0
934	                say(f"--- plateau detected: halving λ → {rate:.6f} ---")
935	            else:
936	                say(f"--- termination: avg improvement < 1% after {MAX_HALVINGS} halvings ---")
937	                break
938	
939	    best = history[-1]
940	
941	    if verbose:
942	        sep = "=" * 72
943	        print()
944	        print(sep)
945	        print(f"Final generation: {best['gen']}")
946	        print(f"Best fitness:     {best['best']:.4f}")
947	        print(f"Avg fitness:      {best['avg']:.4f}")
948	        print(f"Worst fitness:    {best['worst']:.4f}")
949	        print(f"Final λ:          {rate:.6f}")
950	        print(sep)
951	
952	    if write_outputs:
953	        write_best_schedule(best["best_row"], best["best"])
954	        write_history_csv(history)
955	        if verbose:
956	            final_sched = row_to_schedule(best["best_row"])
957	            final_sched.fitness = best["best"]
958	            print("\nBest schedule (sorted by time):")
959	            print_schedule(final_sched, sort_by="time")
960	
961	    best["final_rate"] = rate
962	    best["halving_gens"] = halving_gens
963	    best["history"] = history
964	    return best
965	
966	
967	def run_many(n_runs: int,
968	             max_generations: Optional[int] = None,
969	             base_seed: int = 0) -> dict:
970	    # Run the GA n_runs times with distinct seeds; report the overall best.
971	    import time
972	    print(f"Headless batch: {n_runs} independent GA runs (seeds {base_seed}..{base_seed + n_runs - 1})")
973	    print("-" * 72)
974	    bests: list[float] = []
975	    gens:  list[int]   = []
976	    times: list[float] = []
977	    overall_best: Optional[dict] = None
978	    overall_seed: Optional[int] = None
979	    batch_start = time.time()
980	    for i in range(n_runs):
981	        seed = base_seed + i
982	        t0 = time.time()
983	        result = run_ga(
984	            seed=seed,
985	            verbose=False,
986	            max_generations=max_generations,
987	            write_outputs=False,
988	        )
989	        elapsed = time.time() - t0
990	        bests.append(result["best"])
991	        gens.append(result["gen"])
992	        times.append(elapsed)
993	        flag = ""
994	        if overall_best is None or result["best"] > overall_best["best"]:
995	            overall_best = result
996	            overall_seed = seed
997	            flag = "  ← new best"
998	        print(f"  Run {i+1:>3}/{n_runs} | seed={seed:>4} | gen={result['gen']:>4} | "
999	              f"best={result['best']:7.3f} | time={elapsed:5.1f}s{flag}")
1000	    total = time.time() - batch_start
1001	    bests_arr = np.array(bests)
1002	    gens_arr  = np.array(gens)
1003	
1004	    sep = "=" * 72
1005	    print()
1006	    print(sep)
1007	    print(f"Batch summary  ({n_runs} runs, total wall time {total:.1f}s)")
1008	    print(sep)
1009	    print(f"  Best fitness:    {bests_arr.max():.4f}  (seed={overall_seed})")
1010	    print(f"  Mean fitness:    {bests_arr.mean():.4f}")
1011	    print(f"  Median fitness:  {float(np.median(bests_arr)):.4f}")
1012	    print(f"  Worst fitness:   {bests_arr.min():.4f}")
1013	    print(f"  Std dev:         {bests_arr.std():.4f}")
1014	    print(f"  Mean gens to stop: {gens_arr.mean():.1f}  (min {gens_arr.min()}, max {gens_arr.max()})")
1015	    print(sep)
1016	
1017	    # Write the overall winner separately and a CSV of per-run stats.
1018	    write_best_schedule(overall_best["best_row"], overall_best["best"], path="best_of_runs.txt")
1019	    with open("runs_summary.csv", "w", newline="") as f:
1020	        w = csv.writer(f)
1021	        w.writerow(["run", "seed", "gen", "best", "time_s"])
1022	        for i, (b, g, t) in enumerate(zip(bests, gens, times)):
1023	            w.writerow([i + 1, base_seed + i, g, b, t])
1024	    print("Wrote runs_summary.csv")
1025	
1026	    final_sched = row_to_schedule(overall_best["best_row"])
1027	    final_sched.fitness = overall_best["best"]
1028	    print("\nOverall best schedule (sorted by time):")
1029	    print_schedule(final_sched, sort_by="time")
1030	    return overall_best
1031	
1032	
1033	# End of Part 3
1034	
1035	
1036	def main() -> None:
1037	    import argparse
1038	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="CS461 Program 2 — Genetic Algorithm scheduler")
1039	    parser.add_argument("--viz", action="store_true",
1040	                        help="show live matplotlib visualization (single-run only)")
1041	    parser.add_argument("--runs", type=int, default=1, metavar="N",
1042	                        help="number of independent GA runs (headless batch mode)")
1043	    parser.add_argument("--max-gen", type=int, default=None, metavar="G",
1044	                        help="cap the number of generations (useful for testing)")
1045	    parser.add_argument("--seed", type=int, default=None,
1046	                        help="RNG seed for single-run reproducibility; base seed for --runs")
1047	    args = parser.parse_args()
1048	
1049	    if args.runs > 1:
1050	        if args.viz:
1051	            print("note: --viz is ignored in batch mode (--runs > 1).")
1052	        run_many(args.runs, max_generations=args.max_gen, base_seed=args.seed or 0)
1053	        return
1054	
1055	    viz: Optional[Visualizer] = None
1056	    if args.viz:
1057	        viz = Visualizer()
1058	    try:
1059	        run_ga(max_generations=args.max_gen, seed=args.seed, visualizer=viz)
1060	    finally:
1061	        if viz is not None:
1062	            viz.close(block=True)
1063	
1064	
1065	if __name__ == "__main__":
1066	    main()
1067

## Turn 381 — ASSISTANT — 2026-04-21T15:10:22.869Z
================================================================================
[TEXT]
**Decrease.** The spec explicitly says to halve it.

From the Note on rate:

> "Once your program is running, watch what happens to the fitness score as generations increase. and then cut the mutation (λ/2) rate in half. As long as your results continue to improve, continue cutting the mutation rate in half until things appear to be stable."

So: on plateau → `λ = λ / 2`, repeat until stable. Your code does exactly this at [CS461Program2Test.py:929](CS461Program2Test.py#L929) (`rate /= 2.0`), capped at `MAX_HALVINGS = 4` halvings before termination. Matches the spec.

Note that this is the opposite of the common "adaptive mutation" heuristic (*increase* mutation on plateau to escape local optima) — the spec is deliberately prescribing a cooling schedule instead.

[TEXT]
**Previously was correct. Now it's wrong per the spec.**

Current code at [CS461Program2Test.py:957](CS461Program2Test.py#L957) doubles λ on plateau (`rate * 2.0`, capped at `MAX_MUTATION_RATE = 0.2`). The spec Note on rate explicitly says:

> "cut the mutation (λ/2) rate in half. As long as your results continue to improve, continue cutting the mutation rate in half until things appear to be stable."

The rename to `boosts` / `MAX_BOOSTS` / `last_boost_gen` / `PLATEAU_COOLDOWN` / `MAX_MUTATION_RATE` and the `rate * 2.0` change all push the code in the opposite direction from the spec.

**What changed (needs to be reverted for spec compliance):**
- Line 117 comment: "doubled on plateau" → should be "halved on plateau"
- Line 118: `MAX_MUTATION_RATE = 0.2` ceiling → not needed (halving has no ceiling concern)
- Line 123: `PLATEAU_COOLDOWN` → `HALVING_COOLDOWN`
- Line 124: `MAX_BOOSTS` → `MAX_HALVINGS`
- Line 893–895: `boosts` / `last_boost_gen` / `boost_gens` → `halvings` / `last_halve_gen` / `halving_gens`
- Line 957: `rate = min(MAX_MUTATION_RATE, rate * 2.0)` → `rate /= 2.0`
- Line 962: "boosting λ" → "halving λ"
- Line 964: `MAX_BOOSTS` → `MAX_HALVINGS`
- Line 992: `boost_gens` → `halving_gens`

Want me to revert it?

919	        elite_fit = fitness[elite_idx]
920	
921	        a_idx, b_idx = choose_pair_indices(elite_fit, pair_count, rng)
922	        c1, c2 = crossover_batch(elite_pop[a_idx], elite_pop[b_idx], rng)
923	        offspring = np.concatenate([c1, c2], axis=0)
924	        mutate_batch(offspring, rate, rng)
925	        off_fit = score_batch(offspring)
926	
927	        pop     = np.concatenate([elite_pop, offspring], axis=0)
928	        fitness = np.concatenate([elite_fit,  off_fit],  axis=0)
929	
930	        prev_avg = history[-1]["avg"]
931	        denom = abs(prev_avg) if prev_avg != 0 else 1.0
932	        delta_pct = 100.0 * (fitness.mean() - prev_avg) / denom
933	        snapshot(gen, delta_pct)
934	
935	        assert pop.shape == (pop_size, N_ACTS, 3), f"bad pop shape {pop.shape}"
936	        assert fitness.shape == (pop_size,), f"bad fitness shape {fitness.shape}"
937	        assert not np.isnan(fitness).any(), "fitness contains NaN"
938	
939	        if visualizer is not None:
940	            visualizer.on_gen(history, pop, fitness, rate, boost_gens)
941	
942	        if max_generations is not None and gen >= max_generations:
943	            say(f"--- hit max_generations={max_generations}, stopping ---")
944	            break
945	
946	        if gen < min_generations:
947	            continue
948	
949	        if delta_pct < IMPROVEMENT_THRESHOLD * 100:
950	            streak += 1
951	        else:
952	            streak = 0
953	
954	        if streak >= PLATEAU_DEBOUNCE and (gen - last_boost_gen) >= PLATEAU_COOLDOWN:
955	            if boosts < MAX_BOOSTS:
956	                rate = min(MAX_MUTATION_RATE, rate * 2.0)
957	                boosts += 1
958	                last_boost_gen = gen
959	                boost_gens.append(gen)
960	                streak = 0
961	                say(f"--- plateau detected: boosting λ → {rate:.6f} ---")
962	            else:
963	                say(f"--- termination: avg improvement < 1% after {MAX_BOOSTS} boosts ---")
964	                break

================================================================================

114	POPULATION_SIZE:       int   = 1000   # total schedules per generation

118	SELECTION_TEMPERATURE: float = 2.0    # softmax temperature; higher = flatter selection

129	# DATA STRUCTURES
130	
131	@dataclass
132	class ActivityDef:
133	    """Static definition of an activity (read-only reference data)."""
134	    name:       str
135	    enrollment: int
136	    preferred:  list[str]
137	    other:      list[str]
138	
139	
140	@dataclass
141	class Assignment:
142	    """
143	    A single activity's assignment within one schedule.
144	    When you implement the GA in this can be adjusted
145	    """
146	    activity:    ActivityDef   # reference to the static definition
147	    room:        str           # chosen room name
148	    time:        str           # chosen time slot
149	    facilitator: str           # chosen facilitator name
150	
151	
152	@dataclass
153	class Schedule:
154	    """
155	    One candidate schedule: 11 assignments (one per activity).
156	    fitness is set to None until scored in Part 2
157	    """
158	    assignments: list[Assignment]
159	    fitness:     Optional[float] = field(default=None)
160	
161	    def copy(self) -> "Schedule":
162	        """Return a deep copy suitable for offspring creation."""
163	        new_assignments = [
164	            Assignment(
165	                activity=a.activity,
166	                room=a.room,
167	                time=a.time,
168	                facilitator=a.facilitator,
169	            )
170	            for a in self.assignments
171	        ]
172	        return Schedule(assignments=new_assignments)
173	
174	
175	
176	# RANDOM SCHEDULE GENERATION
177	
178	
179	# Uses NumPy's PCG64DXSM for better random numbers
180	_rng = Generator(PCG64DXSM())
181	
182	# Build ActivityDef objects once
183	ACTIVITY_DEFS: list[ActivityDef] = [
184	    ActivityDef(**d) for d in ACTIVITIES_DEF
185	]
186	
187	
188	def random_assignment(activity_def: ActivityDef) -> Assignment:
189	    """Randomly assigns a room, time, and facilitator to a single activity"""
190	    room        = ROOM_NAMES[_rng.integers(0, len(ROOM_NAMES))]
191	    time        = TIMES[_rng.integers(0, len(TIMES))]
192	    facilitator = FACILITATORS[_rng.integers(0, len(FACILITATORS))]
193	    return Assignment(activity=activity_def, room=room, time=time, facilitator=facilitator)
194	
195	
196	def generate_random_schedule() -> Schedule:
197	    """Creates a fully random schedule covering all 11 activities"""
198	    assignments = [random_assignment(ad) for ad in ACTIVITY_DEFS]
199	    return Schedule(assignments=assignments)
200	
201	
202	def generate_population(size: int = POPULATION_SIZE) -> list[Schedule]:
203	    """Generates an initial population of `size` random schedules, size can be changed above"""
204	    return [generate_random_schedule() for _ in range(size)]
205	
206	
207	
208	# DISPLAY HELPERS
209	
210	def _facilitator_label(assignment: Assignment) -> str:
211	    """Annotate facilitator with (P)referred, (O)ther, or (X) for neither."""
212	    f = assignment.facilitator
213	    if f in assignment.activity.preferred:
214	        return f"{f} (Preferred)"
215	    if f in assignment.activity.other:
216	        return f"{f} (Other)"
217	    return f"{f} (Not Prefered)"
218	
219	
220	def print_schedule(schedule: Schedule, sort_by: str = "time") -> None:
221	    """
222	    Pretty-print a schedule to stdout.
223	
224	    sort_by: "time"     → ordered by time slot then activity name
225	             "activity" → ordered by activity name
226	    """
227	    assignments = schedule.assignments[:]
228	
229	    if sort_by == "time":
230	        time_order = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
231	        assignments.sort(key=lambda a: (time_order[a.time], a.activity.name))
232	        header = "Schedule — sorted by Time Slot"
233	    else:
234	        assignments.sort(key=lambda a: a.activity.name)
235	        header = "Schedule — sorted by Activity"
236	
237	    col_w = [12, 14, 12, 28, 10]   # activity, room, time, facilitator, enrollment
238	    sep   = "─" * (sum(col_w) + len(col_w) * 3 + 1)
239	
240	    print()
241	    print("=" * len(sep))
242	    print(f"  {header}")
243	    print("=" * len(sep))
244	
245	    # column headers
246	    print(
247	        f"  {'Activity':<{col_w[0]}}  "
248	        f"{'Room':<{col_w[1]}}  "
249	        f"{'Time':<{col_w[2]}}  "
250	        f"{'Facilitator':<{col_w[3]}}  "
251	        f"{'Enroll':>{col_w[4]}}"
252	    )
253	    print(sep)
254	
255	    prev_time = None
256	    for a in assignments:
257	        # blank separator between time groups when sorted by time
258	        if sort_by == "time" and a.time != prev_time and prev_time is not None:
259	            print()
260	        prev_time = a.time
261	
262	        cap   = ROOMS[a.room]
263	        enroll = a.activity.enrollment
264	        room_note = ""
265	        if cap < enroll:
266	            room_note = " [TOO SMALL]"
267	        elif cap > 3 * enroll:
268	            room_note = " [>>3x]"
269	        elif cap > 1.5 * enroll:
270	            room_note = " [>1.5x]"
271	
272	        print(
273	            f"  {a.activity.name:<{col_w[0]}}  "
274	            f"{a.room + room_note:<{col_w[1] + len(room_note)}}  "
275	            f"{a.time:<{col_w[2]}}  "
276	            f"{_facilitator_label(a):<{col_w[3]}}  "
277	            f"{enroll:>{col_w[4]}}"
278	        )
279	
280	    print(sep)
281	    if schedule.fitness is not None:
282	        print(f"  Fitness: {schedule.fitness:.4f}")
283	    else:
284	        print("  Fitness: (not yet evaluated)")
285	    print()
286

288	# Start of Part 2
289	
290	
291	# Map each time slot to an index so we can do distance comparisons easily
292	TIME_INDEX: dict[str, int] = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
293	
294	
295	def score_schedule(schedule: Schedule) -> float:
296	    # Scores a single schedule and stores the result in schedule.fitness
297	    # Returns the fitness value. Higher is better.
298	    total = 0.0
299	
300	    # Counts how many times each facilitator appears at each time slot, and how many total activities they're assigned across the schedule
301	    fac_at_time:  dict[str, dict[str, int]] = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(int))
302	    fac_total:    dict[str, int]            = defaultdict(int)
303	    room_at_time: dict[str, dict[str, int]] = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(int))
304	
305	    for a in schedule.assignments:
306	        fac_at_time[a.facilitator][a.time] += 1
307	        fac_total[a.facilitator]           += 1
308	        room_at_time[a.room][a.time]       += 1
309	
310	    for a in schedule.assignments:
311	        cap    = ROOMS[a.room]
312	        enroll = a.activity.enrollment
313	
314	        # Room size scoring
315	        if cap < enroll:
316	            total -= 0.5
317	        elif cap > 3 * enroll:
318	            total -= 0.4
319	        elif cap > 1.5 * enroll:
320	            total -= 0.2
321	        else:
322	            total += 0.3
323	
324	        # Two activities booked in the same room at the same time
325	        if room_at_time[a.room][a.time] > 1:
326	            total -= 0.5
327	
328	        # Facilitator preference
329	        if a.facilitator in a.activity.preferred:
330	            total += 0.5
331	        elif a.facilitator in a.activity.other:
332	            total += 0.2
333	        else:
334	            total -= 0.1
335	
336	        # Facilitator load in this time slot
337	        if fac_at_time[a.facilitator][a.time] == 1:
338	            total += 0.2
339	        elif fac_at_time[a.facilitator][a.time] > 1:
340	            total -= 0.2
341	
342	    # Penalize or reward based on how many total activities a facilitator teaches
343	    for fac, count in fac_total.items():
344	        if count > 4:
345	            total -= 0.5
346	        elif count < 3:
347	            # Tyler is committee chair: no penalty if he has fewer than 2 activities
348	            if not (fac == "Tyler" and count < 2):
349	                total -= 0.4
350	
351	    # Activity-specific rules for the 101 and 191 sections
352	    by_name: dict[str, Assignment] = {a.activity.name: a for a in schedule.assignments}
353	
354	    sla101a = by_name.get("SLA101A")
355	    sla101b = by_name.get("SLA101B")
356	    sla191a = by_name.get("SLA191A")
357	    sla191b = by_name.get("SLA191B")
358	
359	    # The two SLA101 sections should be spread out
360	    if sla101a and sla101b:
361	        diff = abs(TIME_INDEX[sla101a.time] - TIME_INDEX[sla101b.time])
362	        if diff == 0:
363	            total -= 0.5
364	        elif diff >= 4:
365	            total += 0.5
366	
367	    # Same idea for the two SLA191 sections
368	    if sla191a and sla191b:
369	        diff = abs(TIME_INDEX[sla191a.time] - TIME_INDEX[sla191b.time])
370	        if diff == 0:
371	            total -= 0.5
372	        elif diff >= 4:
373	            total += 0.5
374	
375	    ROMAN_BEACH = {"Roman 201", "Roman 216", "Beach 201", "Beach 301"}
376	
377	    # Reward 101/191 pairs that run back-to-back, penalize if they overlap
378	    for s101 in filter(None, [sla101a, sla101b]):
379	        for s191 in filter(None, [sla191a, sla191b]):
380	            diff = abs(TIME_INDEX[s101.time] - TIME_INDEX[s191.time])
381	            if diff == 0:
382	                total -= 0.25
383	            elif diff == 1:
384	                total += 0.5
385	                # Penalize if one is in Roman/Beach and the other is not (widely separated buildings)
386	                if (s101.room in ROMAN_BEACH) != (s191.room in ROMAN_BEACH):
387	                    total -= 0.4
388	            elif diff == 2:
389	                total += 0.25
390	
391	    # Penalize facilitators with consecutive time slots if their rooms are in different buildings
392	    # (Roman/Beach vs everything else) — same rule as 101/191 consecutive building mismatch
393	    fac_rooms: dict[str, dict[str, str]] = defaultdict(dict)
394	    for a in schedule.assignments:
395	        fac_rooms[a.facilitator][a.time] = a.room
396	
397	    for fac in fac_rooms:
398	        slots = sorted(fac_rooms[fac].keys(), key=lambda t: TIME_INDEX[t])
399	        for i in range(len(slots) - 1):
400	            if TIME_INDEX[slots[i + 1]] - TIME_INDEX[slots[i]] == 1:
401	                room_a = fac_rooms[fac][slots[i]]
402	                room_b = fac_rooms[fac][slots[i + 1]]
403	                if (room_a in ROMAN_BEACH) != (room_b in ROMAN_BEACH):
404	                    total -= 0.4
405	
406	    schedule.fitness = total
407	    return total
408	
409	
410	def score_population(population: list[Schedule]) -> None:
411	    # Scores every schedule in the population (mutates in place)
412	    for s in population:
413	        score_schedule(s)
414	
415	
416	def population_stats(population: list[Schedule]) -> dict:
417	    # Returns best, worst, average fitness and references to the best/worst schedules
418	    scored = [s for s in population if s.fitness is not None]
419	    if not scored:
420	        return {}
421	    fitnesses   = [s.fitness for s in scored]
422	    best_sched  = max(scored, key=lambda s: s.fitness)
423	    worst_sched = min(scored, key=lambda s: s.fitness)
424	    return {
425	        "best":        best_sched.fitness,
426	        "worst":       worst_sched.fitness,
427	        "average":     sum(fitnesses) / len(fitnesses),
428	        "best_sched":  best_sched,
429	        "worst_sched": worst_sched,
430	        "count":       len(scored),
431	    }
432	
433	
434	def print_stats(stats: dict, generation: int = 0, prev_best: float = None) -> None:
435	    # Prints a one-line summary for a generation; shows % improvement if prev_best is given
436	
437	    # NOTE: % improvement will be blank at generation 0 b/c there is nothing to compare to yet. It will start showing once Part 3's evolution loop runs and passes the previous generation's best fitness into prev_best each iteration
438	
439	    pct_str = ""
440	    if prev_best is not None and prev_best != 0:
441	        improvement = (stats["best"] - prev_best) / abs(prev_best) * 100
442	        pct_str = f"  |  Improvement: {improvement:+.2f}%"
443	
444	    print(
445	        f"  Gen {generation:>4}  |  "
446	        f"Best: {stats['best']:>8.4f}  |  "
447	        f"Worst: {stats['worst']:>8.4f}  |  "
448	        f"Avg: {stats['average']:>8.4f}"
449	        + pct_str
450	    )
451	
452	# End of Part 2
453	
454	
455	# Start of Part 3: Genetic Algorithm (NumPy-vectorized)
456	
457	
458	# Index maps and lookup tables (built once at startup)
459	TIME_TO_IDX: dict[str, int] = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
460	ROOM_TO_IDX: dict[str, int] = {r: i for i, r in enumerate(ROOMS)}
461	FAC_TO_IDX:  dict[str, int] = {f: i for i, f in enumerate(FACILITATORS)}
462	ACT_NAMES:   list[str]      = [a["name"] for a in ACTIVITIES_DEF]
463	
464	N_TIMES = len(TIMES)
465	N_ROOMS = len(ROOMS)
466	N_FACS  = len(FACILITATORS)
467	N_ACTS  = len(ACTIVITIES_DEF)
468	
469	ROOM_CAPACITY       = np.array(list(ROOMS.values()), dtype=np.int64)
470	ACTIVITY_ENROLLMENT = np.array([a["enrollment"] for a in ACTIVITIES_DEF], dtype=np.int64)
471	
472	# (11, 10) facilitator score: +0.5 preferred, +0.2 other, -0.1 neither.
473	# `other` is written first so `preferred` overwrites duplicates (e.g. SLA449 lists
474	# Zeldin in both) — matches score_schedule's if/elif order.
475	FAC_SCORE = np.full((N_ACTS, N_FACS), -0.1, dtype=np.float64)
476	for _a_idx, _act in enumerate(ACTIVITIES_DEF):
477	    for _f in _act["other"]:
478	        FAC_SCORE[_a_idx, FAC_TO_IDX[_f]] = 0.2
479	    for _f in _act["preferred"]:
480	        FAC_SCORE[_a_idx, FAC_TO_IDX[_f]] = 0.5
481	
482	ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS = np.array(
483	    [name.startswith(("Roman", "Beach")) for name in ROOMS],
484	    dtype=bool,
485	)
486	
487	IDX_101A = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA101A")
488	IDX_101B = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA101B")
489	IDX_191A = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA191A")
490	IDX_191B = ACT_NAMES.index("SLA191B")
491	TYLER_IDX = FAC_TO_IDX["Tyler"]
492	
493	PAIR_I, PAIR_J = np.triu_indices(N_ACTS, k=1)   # 55 pairs
494	
495	_GA_RNG: Generator = Generator(PCG64DXSM())
496	
497	
498	def random_population_array(n: int, rng: Optional[Generator] = None) -> np.ndarray:
499	    # Generate n random schedules as a single (n, 11, 3) int array.
500	    if rng is None:
501	        rng = _GA_RNG
502	    pop = np.empty((n, N_ACTS, 3), dtype=np.int64)
503	    pop[:, :, 0] = rng.integers(0, N_TIMES, size=(n, N_ACTS))
504	    pop[:, :, 1] = rng.integers(0, N_ROOMS, size=(n, N_ACTS))
505	    pop[:, :, 2] = rng.integers(0, N_FACS,  size=(n, N_ACTS))
506	    return pop
507	
508	
509	def row_to_schedule(row: np.ndarray) -> Schedule:
510	    # Convert a (11, 3) genome row into a Schedule dataclass (for printing).
511	    assignments = []
512	    for a_idx in range(N_ACTS):
513	        t_idx = int(row[a_idx, 0])
514	        r_idx = int(row[a_idx, 1])
515	        f_idx = int(row[a_idx, 2])
516	        assignments.append(Assignment(
517	            activity=ACTIVITY_DEFS[a_idx],
518	            room=ROOM_NAMES[r_idx],
519	            time=TIMES[t_idx],
520	            facilitator=FACILITATORS[f_idx],
521	        ))
522	    return Schedule(assignments=assignments)
523	
524	
525	def score_batch(pop: np.ndarray, return_breakdown: bool = False):
526	    # Vectorized fitness for an (M, 11, 3) population.
527	    # Mirrors score_schedule exactly (verified by parity_test).
528	    # If return_breakdown=True, also returns a dict mapping component name to (M,) array.
529	    M = pop.shape[0]
530	    times = pop[:, :, 0]
531	    rooms = pop[:, :, 1]
532	    facs  = pop[:, :, 2]
533	
534	    # Room size rubric
535	    cap = ROOM_CAPACITY[rooms]
536	    enr = ACTIVITY_ENROLLMENT[None, :]
537	    room_score = np.where(
538	        cap < enr, -0.5,
539	        np.where(cap > 3 * enr, -0.4,
540	        np.where(cap > 1.5 * enr, -0.2, 0.3))
541	    )
542	    room_total = room_score.sum(axis=1)
543	
544	    # Same-time-same-room collisions (any colliding activity: -0.5)
545	    same_time = times[:, PAIR_I] == times[:, PAIR_J]
546	    same_room = rooms[:, PAIR_I] == rooms[:, PAIR_J]
547	    collides  = same_time & same_room
548	    counts = np.zeros((M, N_ACTS), dtype=np.int64)
549	    np.add.at(counts, (slice(None), PAIR_I), collides.astype(np.int64))
550	    np.add.at(counts, (slice(None), PAIR_J), collides.astype(np.int64))
551	    collision_total = (-0.5 * (counts > 0).astype(np.float64)).sum(axis=1)
552	
553	    # Facilitator preference (per-activity lookup)
554	    act_idx = np.arange(N_ACTS)[None, :]
555	    fac_pref_total = FAC_SCORE[act_idx, facs].sum(axis=1)
556	
557	    # Facilitator load per (time, fac)
558	    ft_counts = np.zeros((M, N_TIMES, N_FACS), dtype=np.int64)
559	    np.add.at(ft_counts, (np.arange(M)[:, None], times, facs), 1)
560	    shared = ft_counts[np.arange(M)[:, None], times, facs]
561	    fac_load_total = np.where(shared == 1, 0.2, -0.2).sum(axis=1)
562	
563	    # Global facilitator totals (-0.5 if >4; -0.4 if <3 with Tyler exemption for <2)
564	    f_totals = ft_counts.sum(axis=1)
565	    over_4 = f_totals > 4
566	    under_3 = (f_totals > 0) & (f_totals < 3)
567	    tyler_col = (f_totals[:, TYLER_IDX] >= 2) & (f_totals[:, TYLER_IDX] < 3)
568	    under_3[:, TYLER_IDX] = tyler_col
569	    fac_global_total = -0.5 * over_4.sum(axis=1) - 0.4 * under_3.sum(axis=1)
570	
571	    # SLA 101A vs 101B
572	    d = np.abs(times[:, IDX_101A] - times[:, IDX_101B])
573	    sla_101_total = np.where(d == 0, -0.5, 0.0) + np.where(d >= 4, 0.5, 0.0)
574	
575	    # SLA 191A vs 191B
576	    d = np.abs(times[:, IDX_191A] - times[:, IDX_191B])
577	    sla_191_total = np.where(d == 0, -0.5, 0.0) + np.where(d >= 4, 0.5, 0.0)
578	
579	    # Cross 101 x 191 pairs
580	    sla_cross_total = np.zeros(M, dtype=np.float64)
581	    pairs_101 = [IDX_101A, IDX_101A, IDX_101B, IDX_101B]
582	    pairs_191 = [IDX_191A, IDX_191B, IDX_191A, IDX_191B]
583	    for a_i, a_j in zip(pairs_101, pairs_191):
584	        t_a = times[:, a_i]; t_b = times[:, a_j]
585	        r_a = rooms[:, a_i]; r_b = rooms[:, a_j]
586	        d = np.abs(t_a - t_b)
587	        sla_cross_total += np.where(d == 0, -0.25, 0.0)
588	        sla_cross_total += np.where(d == 1,  0.5,  0.0)
589	        sla_cross_total += np.where(d == 2,  0.25, 0.0)
590	        consec = (d == 1)
591	        rb_a = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_a]
592	        rb_b = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_b]
593	        mismatch = consec & (rb_a != rb_b)
594	        sla_cross_total += np.where(mismatch, -0.4, 0.0)
595	
596	    # Facilitator consecutive slots with building mismatch (-0.4 per occurrence).
597	    # Mirrors score_schedule quirk: last activity in activity-order wins the (time, fac) slot.
598	    fac_room_at_time = np.full((M, N_TIMES, N_FACS), -1, dtype=np.int64)
599	    row_idx = np.arange(M)
600	    for act_i in range(N_ACTS):
601	        fac_room_at_time[row_idx, times[:, act_i], facs[:, act_i]] = rooms[:, act_i]
602	    occupied = fac_room_at_time >= 0
603	    fac_consec_total = np.zeros(M, dtype=np.float64)
604	    for t_slot in range(N_TIMES - 1):
605	        both = occupied[:, t_slot, :] & occupied[:, t_slot + 1, :]
606	        r_a = np.where(both, fac_room_at_time[:, t_slot,     :], 0)
607	        r_b = np.where(both, fac_room_at_time[:, t_slot + 1, :], 0)
608	        rb_a = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_a]
609	        rb_b = ROMAN_BEACH_ROOMS[r_b]
610	        mismatch = both & (rb_a != rb_b)
611	        fac_consec_total += -0.4 * mismatch.sum(axis=1)
612	
613	    fitness = (
614	        room_total + collision_total + fac_pref_total + fac_load_total
615	        + fac_global_total + sla_101_total + sla_191_total
616	        + sla_cross_total + fac_consec_total
617	    )
618	
619	    if return_breakdown:
620	        breakdown = {
621	            "room size":       room_total,
622	            "collisions":      collision_total,
623	            "fac preference":  fac_pref_total,
624	            "fac load (slot)": fac_load_total,
625	            "fac totals":      fac_global_total,
626	            "SLA 101 split":   sla_101_total,
627	            "SLA 191 split":   sla_191_total,
628	            "SLA 101×191":     sla_cross_total,
629	            "fac consecutive": fac_consec_total,
630	        }
631	        return fitness, breakdown
632	    return fitness
633	
634	
635	def parity_test(n: int = 200, seed: int = 0) -> None:
636	    # Assert score_batch matches score_schedule on n random schedules.
637	    rng = Generator(PCG64DXSM(seed=seed))
638	    pop = random_population_array(n, rng=rng)
639	    vec_scores = score_batch(pop)
640	    for i in range(n):
641	        ref = score_schedule(row_to_schedule(pop[i]))
642	        if not np.isclose(vec_scores[i], ref, atol=1e-9):
643	            print(f"Parity mismatch at i={i}: vec={vec_scores[i]} ref={ref}")
644	            print(f"  genome: {pop[i].tolist()}")
645	            raise AssertionError("score_batch does not match score_schedule")
646	    print(f"Parity test passed ({n} schedules).")
647	
648	
649	def crossover_batch(parents_a: np.ndarray, parents_b: np.ndarray,
650	                    rng: Generator) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
651	    # Per-field coin-flip crossover. Returns two child arrays, each (P, 11, 3).
652	    mask = rng.random((parents_a.shape[0], N_ACTS, 3)) < 0.5
653	    child1 = np.where(mask, parents_a, parents_b).astype(np.int64, copy=False)
654	    child2 = np.where(mask, parents_b, parents_a).astype(np.int64, copy=False)
655	    return child1, child2
656	
657	
658	def mutate_batch(genomes: np.ndarray, rate: float, rng: Generator) -> None:
659	    # In-place per-gene mutation. Replaces fields with fresh domain draws.
660	    n = genomes.shape[0]
661	    mask = rng.random((n, N_ACTS, 3)) < rate
662	    if not mask.any():
663	        return
664	    replacements = np.empty_like(genomes)
665	    replacements[:, :, 0] = rng.integers(0, N_TIMES, size=(n, N_ACTS))
666	    replacements[:, :, 1] = rng.integers(0, N_ROOMS, size=(n, N_ACTS))
667	    replacements[:, :, 2] = rng.integers(0, N_FACS,  size=(n, N_ACTS))
668	    genomes[mask] = replacements[mask]
669	
670	
671	def choose_pair_indices(elite_fitness: np.ndarray, n_pairs: int,
672	                        rng: Generator,
673	                        temperature: float = SELECTION_TEMPERATURE) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
674	    # Softmax-weighted sampling within the elite block, with replacement across pairs.
675	    # Raw-fitness softmax is extremely peaked when fitness deltas are O(1+),
676	    # so divide by a temperature before exponentiating to keep the selection pressure sane.
677	    shifted = (elite_fitness - elite_fitness.max()) / max(temperature, 1e-9)
678	    probs = np.exp(shifted)
679	    probs /= probs.sum()
680	    picks = rng.choice(len(elite_fitness), size=n_pairs * 2, replace=True, p=probs)
681	    a_idx = picks[0::2].copy()
682	    b_idx = picks[1::2].copy()
683	    dup = a_idx == b_idx
684	    while dup.any():
685	        b_idx[dup] = rng.choice(len(elite_fitness), size=int(dup.sum()), p=probs)
686	        dup = a_idx == b_idx
687	    return a_idx, b_idx
688	
689	
690	def _gen_line(gen: int, best: float, avg: float, worst: float,
691	              delta_pct: Optional[float], rate: float) -> str:
692	    d = f"{delta_pct:+7.2f}%" if delta_pct is not None else "   —   "
693	    return (f"G {gen:>4} | best={best:7.3f} | avg={avg:7.3f} | "
694	            f"worst={worst:7.3f} | Δavg={d} | λ={rate:.5f}")
695	
696	
697	def write_best_schedule(row: np.ndarray, fitness: float,
698	                        path: str = BEST_SCHEDULE_FILE) -> None:
699	    sched = row_to_schedule(row)
700	    sched.fitness = fitness
701	    time_order = {t: i for i, t in enumerate(TIMES)}
702	    assignments = sorted(sched.assignments,
703	                         key=lambda a: (time_order[a.time], a.activity.name))
704	    lines = [
705	        f"Best schedule — fitness = {fitness:.4f}",
706	        "",
707	        f"{'Activity':<10}  {'Time':<6}  {'Room':<12}  {'Facilitator':<12}  {'Enroll':>6}  {'Cap':>4}",
708	        "-" * 60,
709	    ]
710	    prev_time: Optional[str] = None
711	    for a in assignments:
712	        if prev_time is not None and a.time != prev_time:
713	            lines.append("")
714	        prev_time = a.time
715	        lines.append(
716	            f"{a.activity.name:<10}  {a.time:<6}  {a.room:<12}  "
717	            f"{a.facilitator:<12}  {a.activity.enrollment:>6}  {ROOMS[a.room]:>4}"
718	        )
719	    Path(path).write_text("\n".join(lines) + "\n")
720	    print(f"Wrote best schedule → {path}")
721	
722	
723	def plot_fitness_cli(history: list[dict]) -> None:
724	    # Terminal chart of best/avg/worst fitness per generation using plotext.
725	    try:
726	        import plotext as plt
727	    except ImportError:
728	        print("note: plotext not installed — skipping CLI chart. "
729	              "Install with: pip install plotext")
730	        return
731	    gens  = [h["gen"]   for h in history]
732	    best  = [h["best"]  for h in history]
733	    avg   = [h["avg"]   for h in history]
734	    worst = [h["worst"] for h in history]
735	    plt.clear_figure()
736	    plt.theme("clear")
737	    plt.plot(gens, best,  label="best",  color="cyan")
738	    plt.plot(gens, avg,   label="avg",   color="green")
739	    plt.plot(gens, worst, label="worst", color="red")
740	    plt.title("Fitness over generations")
741	    plt.xlabel("generation")
742	    plt.ylabel("fitness")
743	    plt.plotsize(100, 25)
744	    plt.show()
745	
746	
747	def write_history_csv(history: list[dict], path: str = FITNESS_HISTORY_CSV) -> None:
748	    with open(path, "w", newline="") as f:
749	        w = csv.writer(f)
750	        w.writerow(["gen", "best", "avg", "worst", "delta_pct", "lambda"])
751	        for h in history:
752	            w.writerow([
753	                h["gen"], h["best"], h["avg"], h["worst"],
754	                "" if h["delta_pct"] is None else h["delta_pct"],
755	                h["rate"],
756	            ])
757	    print(f"Wrote fitness history → {path}")
758	
759	
760	class Visualizer:
761	    # Live 6-panel matplotlib view that refreshes each generation.
762	    # Lazily imports matplotlib so the module can run headless without it.
763	    def __init__(self) -> None:
764	        try:
765	            import matplotlib
766	            import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
767	        except ImportError as e:
768	            raise RuntimeError(
769	                "matplotlib is required for --viz. Install with: pip install matplotlib"
770	            ) from e
771	        self._plt = plt
772	        plt.ion()
773	        self.fig, self.axes = plt.subplots(2, 3, figsize=(16, 9))
774	        self.fig.suptitle("GA live visualization", fontsize=14)
775	        try:
776	            self.fig.canvas.manager.set_window_title("GA Live")
777	        except Exception:
778	            pass
779	        plt.show(block=False)
780	
781	    def on_gen(self, history: list[dict], pop: np.ndarray, fitness: np.ndarray,
782	               rate: float, halving_gens: list[int]) -> None:
783	        axes = self.axes
784	        best_i = int(np.argmax(fitness))
785	        best_row = pop[best_i]
786	        gens = [h["gen"] for h in history]
787	
788	        # (0,0) fitness over generations + halving markers
789	        ax = axes[0, 0]; ax.clear()
790	        ax.plot(gens, [h["best"]  for h in history], label="best",  color="#1f77b4")
791	        ax.plot(gens, [h["avg"]   for h in history], label="avg",   color="#2ca02c")
792	        ax.plot(gens, [h["worst"] for h in history], label="worst", color="#d62728")
793	        for g in halving_gens:
794	            ax.axvline(g, color="orange", linestyle="--", alpha=0.6, linewidth=1)
795	        ax.set_title("Fitness over generations")
796	        ax.set_xlabel("generation"); ax.set_ylabel("fitness")
797	        ax.legend(loc="lower right"); ax.grid(alpha=0.3)
798	
799	        # (0,1) lambda schedule
800	        ax = axes[0, 1]; ax.clear()
801	        rates = [h["rate"] for h in history]
802	        ax.step(gens, rates, where="post", color="orange")
803	        ax.set_yscale("log")
804	        ax.set_title("Mutation rate λ"); ax.set_xlabel("generation")
805	        ax.set_ylabel("λ (log)"); ax.grid(alpha=0.3)
806	
807	        # (0,2) constraint breakdown of current best
808	        ax = axes[0, 2]; ax.clear()
809	        _, breakdown = score_batch(best_row[None, :, :], return_breakdown=True)
810	        labels = list(breakdown.keys())
811	        values = [float(breakdown[k][0]) for k in labels]
812	        colors = ["#2ca02c" if v >= 0 else "#d62728" for v in values]
813	        ax.barh(labels, values, color=colors)
814	        ax.axvline(0, color="black", linewidth=0.5)
815	        ax.set_title(f"Best breakdown (total = {float(fitness[best_i]):.2f})")
816	        ax.set_xlabel("points"); ax.invert_yaxis()
817	
818	        # (1,0) facilitator load of current best
819	        ax = axes[1, 0]; ax.clear()
820	        counts = np.bincount(best_row[:, 2], minlength=N_FACS)
821	        bar_colors = []
822	        for f_i, c in enumerate(counts):
823	            if c > 4:
824	                bar_colors.append("#d62728")
825	            elif c < 3 and not (f_i == TYLER_IDX and c < 2):
826	                bar_colors.append("#ff7f0e")
827	            else:
828	                bar_colors.append("#2ca02c")
829	        ax.bar(FACILITATORS, counts, color=bar_colors)
830	        ax.axhline(3, color="gray", linestyle=":", alpha=0.6)
831	        ax.axhline(4, color="gray", linestyle=":", alpha=0.6)
832	        ax.set_title("Facilitator load (best)"); ax.set_ylabel("# activities")
833	        ax.tick_params(axis="x", rotation=30)
834	
835	        # (1,1) room utilization of current best
836	        ax = axes[1, 1]; ax.clear()
837	        slot_counts = np.bincount(best_row[:, 1], minlength=N_ROOMS)
838	        ax.bar(ROOM_NAMES, slot_counts, color="#1f77b4")
839	        ax.set_title("Room utilization (best)"); ax.set_ylabel("activities scheduled")
840	        ax.tick_params(axis="x", rotation=30)
841	
842	        # (1,2) time x room heatmap — visualizes same-time-same-room collisions
843	        ax = axes[1, 2]; ax.clear()
844	        heat = np.zeros((N_TIMES, N_ROOMS), dtype=int)
845	        for t, r in zip(best_row[:, 0], best_row[:, 1]):
846	            heat[t, r] += 1
847	        ax.imshow(heat, aspect="auto", cmap="YlOrRd", vmin=0, vmax=max(2, heat.max()))
848	        ax.set_xticks(range(N_ROOMS)); ax.set_xticklabels(ROOM_NAMES, rotation=30, ha="right")
849	        ax.set_yticks(range(N_TIMES)); ax.set_yticklabels(TIMES)
850	        ax.set_title("Time × room (best)")
851	        for (y, x), v in np.ndenumerate(heat):
852	            if v > 0:
853	                ax.text(x, y, str(v), ha="center", va="center",
854	                        color="black" if v < 2 else "white", fontsize=8)
855	
856	        self.fig.tight_layout(rect=[0, 0, 1, 0.96])
857	        self._plt.pause(0.001)
858	
859	    def close(self, block: bool = True) -> None:
860	        self._plt.ioff()
861	        if block:
862	            self._plt.show()
863	
864	
865	def run_ga(pop_size: int = POPULATION_SIZE,
866	           elite_count: int = ELITE_COUNT,
867	           pair_count: int  = PAIR_COUNT,
868	           initial_rate: float = MUTATION_RATE,
869	           min_generations: int = MIN_GENERATIONS,
870	           max_generations: Optional[int] = None,
871	           seed: Optional[int] = None,
872	           verbose: bool = True,
873	           visualizer: Optional[Visualizer] = None,
874	           write_outputs: bool = True) -> dict:
875	    # Main GA loop. Returns the final history snapshot (best-so-far at termination).
876	    rng = Generator(PCG64DXSM(seed=seed)) if seed is not None else _GA_RNG
877	
878	    def say(msg: str) -> None:
879	        if verbose:
880	            print(msg)
881	
882	    if verbose:
883	        say("Parity test: score_batch vs score_schedule …")
884	        parity_test(200)
885	
886	    say(f"Generating initial population of {pop_size} …")
887	    pop = random_population_array(pop_size, rng)
888	    fitness = score_batch(pop)
889	
890	    rate = initial_rate
891	    history: list[dict] = []
892	    halving_gens: list[int] = []
893	    halvings = 0
894	    last_halve_gen = 0
895	    streak = 0
896	
897	    def snapshot(gen: int, delta_pct: Optional[float]) -> None:
898	        best_i = int(np.argmax(fitness))
899	        stats = {
900	            "gen": gen,
901	            "best":  float(fitness.max()),
902	            "avg":   float(fitness.mean()),
903	            "worst": float(fitness.min()),
904	            "delta_pct": delta_pct,
905	            "rate": rate,
906	            "best_row": pop[best_i].copy(),
907	        }
908	        history.append(stats)
909	        if verbose:
910	            print(_gen_line(gen, stats["best"], stats["avg"], stats["worst"], delta_pct, rate))
911	
912	    snapshot(0, None)
913	    if visualizer is not None:
914	        visualizer.on_gen(history, pop, fitness, rate, halving_gens)
915	
916	    for gen in itertools.count(1):
917	        elite_idx = np.argpartition(fitness, -elite_count)[-elite_count:]
918	        elite_pop = pop[elite_idx]
919	        elite_fit = fitness[elite_idx]
920	
921	        a_idx, b_idx = choose_pair_indices(elite_fit, pair_count, rng)
922	        c1, c2 = crossover_batch(elite_pop[a_idx], elite_pop[b_idx], rng)
923	        offspring = np.concatenate([c1, c2], axis=0)
924	        mutate_batch(offspring, rate, rng)
925	        off_fit = score_batch(offspring)
926	
927	        pop     = np.concatenate([elite_pop, offspring], axis=0)
928	        fitness = np.concatenate([elite_fit,  off_fit],  axis=0)
929	
930	        prev_avg = history[-1]["avg"]
931	        denom = abs(prev_avg) if prev_avg != 0 else 1.0
932	        delta_pct = 100.0 * (fitness.mean() - prev_avg) / denom
933	        snapshot(gen, delta_pct)
934	
935	        assert pop.shape == (pop_size, N_ACTS, 3), f"bad pop shape {pop.shape}"
936	        assert fitness.shape == (pop_size,), f"bad fitness shape {fitness.shape}"
937	        assert not np.isnan(fitness).any(), "fitness contains NaN"
938	
939	        if visualizer is not None:
940	            visualizer.on_gen(history, pop, fitness, rate, halving_gens)
941	
942	        if max_generations is not None and gen >= max_generations:
943	            say(f"--- hit max_generations={max_generations}, stopping ---")
944	            break
945	
946	        if gen < min_generations:
947	            continue
948	
949	        if delta_pct < IMPROVEMENT_THRESHOLD * 100:
950	            streak += 1
951	        else:
952	            streak = 0
953	
954	        if streak >= PLATEAU_DEBOUNCE and (gen - last_halve_gen) >= HALVING_COOLDOWN:
955	            if halvings < MAX_HALVINGS:
956	                rate /= 2.0
957	                halvings += 1
958	                last_halve_gen = gen
959	                halving_gens.append(gen)
960	                streak = 0
961	                say(f"--- plateau detected: halving λ → {rate:.6f} ---")
962	            else:
963	                say(f"--- termination: avg improvement < 1% after {MAX_HALVINGS} halvings ---")
964	                break
965	
966	    best = history[-1]
967	
968	    if verbose:
969	        sep = "=" * 72
970	        print()
971	        print(sep)
972	        print(f"Final generation: {best['gen']}")
973	        print(f"Best fitness:     {best['best']:.4f}")
974	        print(f"Avg fitness:      {best['avg']:.4f}")
975	        print(f"Worst fitness:    {best['worst']:.4f}")
976	        print(f"Final λ:          {rate:.6f}")
977	        print(sep)
978	
979	    if write_outputs:
980	        write_best_schedule(best["best_row"], best["best"])
981	        write_history_csv(history)
982	        if verbose:
983	            final_sched = row_to_schedule(best["best_row"])
984	            final_sched.fitness = best["best"]
985	            print("\nBest schedule (sorted by time):")
986	            print_schedule(final_sched, sort_by="time")
987	            if visualizer is None:
988	                plot_fitness_cli(history)
989	
990	    best["final_rate"] = rate
991	    best["halving_gens"] = halving_gens
992	    best["history"] = history
993	    return best
994	
995	
996	def run_many(n_runs: int,
997	             max_generations: Optional[int] = None,
998	             base_seed: int = 0) -> dict:
999	    # Run the GA n_runs times with distinct seeds; report the overall best.
1000	    import time
1001	    print(f"Headless batch: {n_runs} independent GA runs (seeds {base_seed}..{base_seed + n_runs - 1})")
1002	    print("-" * 72)
1003	    bests: list[float] = []
1004	    gens:  list[int]   = []
1005	    times: list[float] = []
1006	    overall_best: Optional[dict] = None
1007	    overall_seed: Optional[int] = None
1008	    batch_start = time.time()
1009	    for i in range(n_runs):
1010	        seed = base_seed + i
1011	        t0 = time.time()
1012	        result = run_ga(
1013	            seed=seed,
1014	            verbose=False,
1015	            max_generations=max_generations,
1016	            write_outputs=False,
1017	        )
1018	        elapsed = time.time() - t0
1019	        bests.append(result["best"])
1020	        gens.append(result["gen"])
1021	        times.append(elapsed)
1022	        flag = ""
1023	        if overall_best is None or result["best"] > overall_best["best"]:
1024	            overall_best = result
1025	            overall_seed = seed
1026	            flag = "  ← new best"
1027	        print(f"  Run {i+1:>3}/{n_runs} | seed={seed:>4} | gen={result['gen']:>4} | "
1028	              f"best={result['best']:7.3f} | time={elapsed:5.1f}s{flag}")
1029	    total = time.time() - batch_start
1030	    bests_arr = np.array(bests)
1031	    gens_arr  = np.array(gens)
1032	
1033	    sep = "=" * 72
1034	    print()
1035	    print(sep)
1036	    print(f"Batch summary  ({n_runs} runs, total wall time {total:.1f}s)")
1037	    print(sep)
1038	    print(f"  Best fitness:    {bests_arr.max():.4f}  (seed={overall_seed})")
1039	    print(f"  Mean fitness:    {bests_arr.mean():.4f}")
1040	    print(f"  Median fitness:  {float(np.median(bests_arr)):.4f}")
1041	    print(f"  Worst fitness:   {bests_arr.min():.4f}")
1042	    print(f"  Std dev:         {bests_arr.std():.4f}")
1043	    print(f"  Mean gens to stop: {gens_arr.mean():.1f}  (min {gens_arr.min()}, max {gens_arr.max()})")
1044	    print(sep)
1045	
1046	    # Write the overall winner separately and a CSV of per-run stats.
1047	    write_best_schedule(overall_best["best_row"], overall_best["best"], path="best_of_runs.txt")
1048	    with open("runs_summary.csv", "w", newline="") as f:
1049	        w = csv.writer(f)
1050	        w.writerow(["run", "seed", "gen", "best", "time_s"])
1051	        for i, (b, g, t) in enumerate(zip(bests, gens, times)):
1052	            w.writerow([i + 1, base_seed + i, g, b, t])
1053	    print("Wrote runs_summary.csv")
1054	
1055	    final_sched = row_to_schedule(overall_best["best_row"])
1056	    final_sched.fitness = overall_best["best"]
1057	    print("\nOverall best schedule (sorted by time):")
1058	    print_schedule(final_sched, sort_by="time")
1059	    return overall_best
1060	
1061	
1062	# End of Part 3
1063	
1064	
1065	def main() -> None:
1066	    import argparse
1067	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="CS461 Program 2 — Genetic Algorithm scheduler")
1068	    parser.add_argument("--viz", action="store_true",
1069	                        help="show live matplotlib visualization (single-run only)")
1070	    parser.add_argument("--runs", type=int, default=1, metavar="N",
1071	                        help="number of independent GA runs (headless batch mode)")
1072	    parser.add_argument("--max-gen", type=int, default=None, metavar="G",
1073	                        help="cap the number of generations (useful for testing)")
1074	    parser.add_argument("--seed", type=int, default=None,
1075	                        help="RNG seed for single-run reproducibility; base seed for --runs")
1076	    args = parser.parse_args()
1077	
1078	    if args.runs > 1:
1079	        if args.viz:
1080	            print("note: --viz is ignored in batch mode (--runs > 1).")
1081	        run_many(args.runs, max_generations=args.max_gen, base_seed=args.seed or 0)
1082	        return
1083	
1084	    viz: Optional[Visualizer] = None
1085	    if args.viz:
1086	        viz = Visualizer()
1087	    try:
1088	        run_ga(max_generations=args.max_gen, seed=args.seed, visualizer=viz)
1089	    finally:
1090	        if viz is not None:
1091	            viz.close(block=True)
1092	
1093	
1094	if __name__ == "__main__":
1095	    main()
1096
